    SELECT r.\"Id\", r.\"FechaBaja\", r.\"Name\"
    FROM \"Roles\" AS r
    WHERE (r.\"FechaBaja\" IS NULL) AND r.\"Id\" = @__id_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT r0.\"MethodId\", r0.\"RoleId\", t1.\"Id\", t1.\"FechaBaja\", t1.\"IdMicroservice\", t1.\"Path\", t1.\"Verb\"
    FROM \"RoleMethod\" AS r0
    INNER JOIN (
        SELECT m.\"Id\", m.\"FechaBaja\", m.\"IdMicroservice\", m.\"Path\", m.\"Verb\"
        FROM \"Methods\" AS m
        WHERE m.\"FechaBaja\" IS NULL
    ) AS t1 ON r0.\"MethodId\" = t1.\"Id\"
) AS t0 ON t.\"Id\" = t0.\"RoleId\"
ORDER BY t.\"Id\", t0.\"MethodId\", t0.\"RoleId\""
